(herald "UAF using TLS1.2 without channel binding.")

(comment "CPSA 4.4.2")
(comment "All input read from uaf-endpoint-tls12.scm")

(defprotocol uaf-unbound-tls12 basic
  (defrole client-reg
    (vars (username auth server ca appid name) (challenge text)
      (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole client-auth
    (vars (server ca appid name) (challenge text) (cr sr random32)
      (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc appid challenge (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash appid
            (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
              (hash server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
            challenge)
          (enc
            (hash appid
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
              challenge) (invk authk))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole server-reg
    (vars (username auth server ca appid name) (challenge text)
      (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (recv cr)
      (send
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (recv
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole server-auth
    (vars (server ca appid name) (challenge text) (cr sr random32)
      (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (recv cr)
      (send
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (recv
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc appid challenge (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash appid
            (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
              (hash server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
            challenge)
          (enc
            (hash appid
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
              challenge) (invk authk))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_indx
    (forall ((x indx)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_strd
    (forall ((x strd)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_mesg
    (forall ((x mesg)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (lang (random32 atom) (random48 atom)))

(defskeleton uaf-unbound-tls12
  (vars (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (challenge text) (authk akey)
    (server ca username auth appid name))
  (defstrand client-reg 6 (cr cr) (sr sr) (pms pms)
    (challenge challenge) (authk authk) (username username) (auth auth)
    (server server) (ca ca) (appid appid))
  (non-orig (invk authk) (privk server) (privk ca))
  (uniq-orig cr sr pms)
  (traces
    ((send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (label 0)
  (unrealized (0 1) (0 3) (0 4))
  (origs (cr (0 0)) (pms (0 2)))
  (comment "1 in cohort - 1 not yet seen"))

(defskeleton uaf-unbound-tls12
  (vars (cr sr cr-0 sr-0 random32) (pms random48) (challenge text)
    (authk akey) (server ca username auth appid name))
  (defstrand client-reg 6 (cr cr) (sr sr) (pms pms)
    (challenge challenge) (authk authk) (username username) (auth auth)
    (server server) (ca ca) (appid appid))
  (defstrand server-auth 2 (cr cr-0) (sr sr-0) (server server) (ca ca))
  (precedes ((1 1) (0 1)))
  (non-orig (invk authk) (privk server) (privk ca))
  (uniq-orig cr sr pms)
  (operation encryption-test (added-strand server-auth 2)
    (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)) (0 1))
  (traces
    ((send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
    ((recv cr-0)
      (send
        (cat sr-0 server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
  (label 1)
  (parent 0)
  (unrealized (0 3) (0 4))
  (comment "3 in cohort - 3 not yet seen"))

(defskeleton uaf-unbound-tls12
  (vars (cr sr cr-0 sr-0 random32) (pms random48) (challenge text)
    (authk akey) (server ca username auth appid name))
  (defstrand client-reg 6 (cr cr) (sr sr) (pms pms)
    (challenge challenge) (authk authk) (username username) (auth auth)
    (server server) (ca ca) (appid appid))
  (defstrand server-auth 2 (cr cr-0) (sr sr-0) (server server) (ca ca))
  (deflistener (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write"))
  (precedes ((1 1) (0 1)) ((2 1) (0 3)))
  (non-orig (invk authk) (privk server) (privk ca))
  (uniq-orig cr sr pms)
  (operation encryption-test
    (added-listener (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write"))
    (enc
      (hash pms "server finished"
        (hash cr sr
          (cat server (pubk server)
            (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
          (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")) (0 3))
  (traces
    ((send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
    ((recv cr-0)
      (send
        (cat sr-0 server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
    ((recv (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write"))
      (send (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write"))))
  (label 4)
  (parent 1)
  (unrealized (0 3) (2 0))
  (comment "1 in cohort - 1 not yet seen"))

(defskeleton uaf-unbound-tls12
  (vars (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (challenge text) (authk akey)
    (username auth appid server ca name))
  (defstrand client-reg 6 (cr cr) (sr sr) (pms pms)
    (challenge challenge) (authk authk) (username username) (auth auth)
    (server server) (ca ca) (appid appid))
  (defstrand server-reg 5 (cr cr) (sr sr) (pms pms)
    (challenge challenge) (username username) (server server) (ca ca)
    (appid appid))
  (precedes ((0 0) (1 0)) ((0 2) (1 2)) ((1 1) (0 1)) ((1 3) (0 3))
    ((1 4) (0 4)))
  (non-orig (invk authk) (privk server) (privk ca))
  (uniq-orig cr sr pms)
  (operation encryption-test (displaced 1 2 server-reg 5)
    (enc username appid challenge
      (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")) (0 4))
  (traces
    ((send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"

                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))

        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))

  (deflistener (cat (hash pms cr sr) "server_write"))
  (precedes ((1 1) (0 1)) ((2 1) (0 3)) ((3 1) (2 0)))
  (non-orig (invk authk) (privk server) (privk ca))
  (uniq-orig cr sr pms)

    (added-listener (cat (hash pms cr sr) "server_write"))
    (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write") (2 0))

          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))

            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))

(defprotocol uaf-unbound-tls12 basic
  (defrole client-reg
    (vars (username auth server ca appid name) (challenge text)
      (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole client-auth
    (vars (server ca appid name) (challenge text) (cr sr random32)
      (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc appid challenge (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash appid

              (hash server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
            challenge)
          (enc
            (hash appid
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
              challenge) (invk authk))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))

(defprotocol uaf-unbound-tls12 basic
  (defrole client-reg
    (vars (username auth server ca appid name) (challenge text)
      (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole client-auth
    (vars (server ca appid name) (challenge text) (cr sr random32)
      (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc appid challenge (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash appid
            (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
              (hash server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
            challenge)
          (enc
            (hash appid
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
              challenge) (invk authk))

                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc appid challenge (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash appid
            (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
              (hash server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
            challenge)
          (enc
            (hash appid
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
              challenge) (invk authk))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_indx
    (forall ((x indx)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_strd
    (forall ((x strd)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_mesg
    (forall ((x mesg)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (lang (random32 atom) (random48 atom)))

  (defrole client-reg
    (vars (username auth server ca appid name) (challenge text)
      (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (authk akey))

        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))

                    (enc pms (pubk server))))

          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))

        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))

(defprotocol uaf-unbound-tls12 basic
  (defrole client-reg
    (vars (username auth server ca appid name) (challenge text)
      (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole client-auth
    (vars (server ca appid name) (challenge text) (cr sr random32)
      (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)

  (defrole server-reg

(defprotocol uaf-unbound-tls12 basic
  (defrole client-reg
    (vars (username auth server ca appid name) (challenge text)
      (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole client-auth
    (vars (server ca appid name) (challenge text) (cr sr random32)
      (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (send cr)
      (recv
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (send
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc appid challenge (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash appid
            (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
              (hash server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
            challenge)
          (enc
            (hash appid
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
              challenge) (invk authk))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole server-reg
    (vars (username auth server ca appid name) (challenge text)
      (cr sr random32) (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (recv cr)
      (send
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (recv
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc username appid challenge
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc (hash "key handle" (invk authk) username)
          (cat auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))))
          (enc auth authk
            (hash appid challenge
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))))
            (invk authk)) (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defrole server-auth
    (vars (server ca appid name) (challenge text) (cr sr random32)
      (pms random48) (authk akey))
    (trace (recv cr)
      (send
        (cat sr server (pubk server)
          (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
      (recv
        (cat (enc pms (pubk server))
          (enc
            (hash pms "client finished"
              (hash cr sr
                (cat server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr
              (cat server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
              (enc pms (pubk server))
              (enc
                (hash pms "client finished"
                  (hash cr sr
                    (cat server (pubk server)
                      (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))
                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (send
        (enc appid challenge (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
      (recv
        (enc
          (hash appid
            (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
              (hash server (pubk server)
                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
            challenge)
          (enc
            (hash appid
              (hash "uaf_server_endpoint" challenge
                (hash server (pubk server)
                  (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca))))
              challenge) (invk authk))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write")))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_indx
    (forall ((x indx)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_strd
    (forall ((x strd)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (defgenrule neqRl_mesg
    (forall ((x mesg)) (implies (fact neq x x) (false))))
  (lang (random32 atom) (random48 atom)))

        (authk akey) (z strd))

        (and (p "server-auth" z 6) (p "server-auth" "sr" z sr)
          (p "server-auth" "challenge" z challenge)

          (uniq-at challenge z 4) (uniq-at sr z 1))
        (exists ((z-0 strd))
          (and (p "client-auth" z-0 6)
            (p "client-auth" "challenge" z-0 challenge)
            (p "client-auth" "server" z-0 server)
            (p "client-auth" "appid" z-0 appid))))))

                (enc pms (pubk server))))
            (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
      (send
        (enc
          (hash pms "server finished"
            (hash cr sr

                (enc (hash server (pubk server)) (privk ca)))

                (hash pms "client finished"

                    (enc pms (pubk server))))
                (hash (hash pms cr sr) "client_write"))))
          (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))

        (enc appid challenge (hash (hash pms cr sr) "server_write")))
